mame2003 per-game video output color format and copy status
======================================================================

FORMAT (per loaded game, default options)
----------------------------------------------------------------------
  VIDEO_RGB_DIRECT + (6BITS or VECTOR) -> 32bpp -> XRGB8888
  VIDEO_RGB_DIRECT (otherwise)         -> 15bpp -> RGB565
  paletted + 6BITS                      -> 16bpp -> XRGB8888
  paletted (otherwise)                  -> 16bpp -> RGB565

COPY STATUS (third column)
----------------------------------------------------------------------
  ZERO-COPY                   pointer handed straight from the game bitmap
                              to the frontend; no conversion, no copy. Only
                              32bpp games drawn upright (ROT0).
  ZERO-COPY|else CONVERT+SWAP 32bpp rotated 90/270: zero-copy when the
                              frontend performs the rotation (RetroArch does
                              by default); only if it can't does mame rotate
                              internally (one swap-convert pass).
  ZERO-COPY|else CONVERT(flip)same, for 180-degree (flip, no swap).
  CONVERT(32bpp flip/swap)    32bpp with a lone flip/swap the frontend's
                              rotation enum can't express; always internal.
  CONVERT(pal->565/8888)      paletted: the game stores palette INDICES, not
                              colors, so an index->RGB lookup is mandatory.
                              This is one pass, written straight into the
                              frontend framebuffer when available -- it is
                              emulation work, not a removable buffer copy.
  CONVERT(1555->565)          direct 15bpp up-converted with one shift/pixel.

SUMMARY (of 4589 games)
----------------------------------------------------------------------
  always zero-copy ............... 254  (32bpp, ROT0)
  zero-copy if frontend rotates ..  37  (32bpp, ROT90/180/270)
  convert once (palette) ........ 4296  (index->RGB, mandatory)
  convert once (1555->565) .......   1
  convert (32bpp odd orientation)    1
